Achó
6

not yet; as acho aban ja ing, rummies mammabas, I do not yet know it, by and bye I shall know it; witten also achai, and achipa

Achoû

足夠

enough

Adam
6

一種比烏鴉小型的鳥

a certain small bird, less than a sparrow; variegated with a long tail; from whose cry future good or bad fortune may be presumed: if it cries out twice, or four times, it betokens misfortune; but if once, or thrice, or five times, then good success; if anything above this, it initiates a still greater blessing, according to the number of cries.

Ada
7

部分

a part or share; from mada, to divide

Adach
7

一條珊瑚鏈； 它的材料可能很差，但很受當地人的喜愛

a coral chain; it may be of poor materials, but much prized by the natives

Adaûdón
7

屋頂

the roof the house

Adda
7

稻田

paddy; used for that production in its various stages. Numatojóarien, as it just shoots forth. Minochûrgaro, as it puts forth a broad leaf. Tummaabbi-alallabach, as it has two leaflets on the side, and one on the top; a resemblance being supposed to lallabach, a green leek. Madocka jû adda, as it is now, 1+1/2 or 2 spans high: gûmmasor, túmmûbaron summatis, when it has attained its full length. Tummedinnid, when the grain begins to form. Pûikon ja adda, when the grain is perfect and hangs bent down. Tummaberook ja adda, when the grain is half ripe and nearly scorched.

Addud
7

一塊

a piece; adda o ariem, a piece of a lemon: from paddat, to cut or break.

Addas and Addas o rima

手掌

the palm of the hand

Aggan

螃蟹

a crab

Agû

各種發射性武器 (標槍、長茅)

all kinds of missile weapons, as javelins, pikes: &c. from magga, to cast

Agganak

結束 終點

seems to mean, it is done, when any end is reached

Ai

這裡、距離不遠之處

seems that, here, but not far off; ai-i, ai-ies, ai-inies, ailo, ailo-ies, and ailemons, the same

Aiag

蟑螂

a cockroach

Aicho and aicho-ies

那裏、距離不遠 之處

there, but not far off. Aicho, aichoies, soo aicho echies, yonder. Pait o ta, so-o roman kallach, gannumma, there, beyond, yonder. Paia innai maro maicho, and mai-hoies, it is so, there it is.

Aicho-ech

在視線之外

beyond, outside, far out of sight

Aisênnas

小星星

small stars

A-i-ór

下列

the following; a-i-or natta, the next; ajor narroa, &c. A-i-or a mato, next after the large one, that is smaller.

Airo and essuro

猜想

to suppose, to imagine.

Aissen,

is frequently used in different senses; if we meet with this expression alone, it seems to intimate the doing away with anything, as when anything is burnt: aissen o chau, it is burnt in the fire; aissen o cho, some one has taken it away.

Aissillak

as chadsja pila, nearly hit

Aito-ilo

seven and seven, by seven

Ake

a word of excuse, when you unknowingly run against any one; as pray excuse me.

Akeraúso

a form of complaint, when any thing falls down

Akobos

a hunting net, placed in the field, to catch beasts; from pakobor, to catch in a net

Allû

show finery, ornament; from Malla or Pallo, to set one's self off.

Alla-a

by and bye

Alldóch

called in the south, kalladóch, a sort of red beans, which the natives wear round their necks, instead of coral beads; they are very posonous.

Alla

that, in order that

Al-ûl

kindness; from ma-allal, to be kind

Alûm

all kinds of projeciles or missle weapons; from Malam, to fight with missle weapons.

Alle

a basket , also a werd used in addressing children

Allecho, or alleicho

added to a word betokens doing or suffering; it also refers to the future. Súmmada, allecho na-amai, which is the same as sunmada na-a mamai, tomorrow I will come

Allolo

fire-wood; as marach o ûllolo, go and get some fire-wood.

Aliod

a barri, a whirlwind

Ami

a prohibitory expression, as ûmi a mochan, bring no food; ûmi a maú a dat-ai, do not pick it.

Amisûn

the north. Matamis-mi-ma, northward. Patamis, transit.

Amo

a plum, a plum tree

Amorra

the liver

Ani

before this. ago; ani rúmmies, in former days; ani zchieta rummies, ten days ago; aninaspaat ai das, four months ago; ani tarnacho a baas, nine years ago: animúnma, and anibanno, when did it happen? People say in the evening; ani mûrpesa, yesterday, or last evening: ani naassa, a little while ago; anissima, this morning early: annach, certainly, verily: ansia, yesterday: ansiûtta, the day before yesterday: ani bi-ini, and anbini, last night: anibaas, last year: ani mossa, like anibaas, like anibaas: animilip, a long time ago: aniaicho, d'cicin ani, a very long since.

Annomûnnoma

go on, go forward: anno man noma taitum madp, get to work; maibas pattillo ta-i, ta-i man, maibas channa, Pray eat.

Annúma

as mumma annuma; Sassonoe, what are you grumbling about.

A-o

pickle

A-orran

maorran, ino-a-orran, fuddled with drinking, sick; people also say madich a mairab a-orran ja ina.

Chummacho
42

擦亮；磨（刀）；磨亮

chinummacho, chachummacho, g. chacho-o, I. chachon, chinûcho, inochach-on, to polish. Pachacho, to polish, &c. Cho chummacho; inochachon, bato achoan; the man polishes; the knife is whetted; the stone grinds it sharp. Chachach-o, a grinding; ma-acha *cha_h-o, a grindstone.

Chûmmadik
42

接近；靠近

chi, cha, chaddikka, chûddikken, chinaddik, ino-chàddikken, to approach. Pachaddik, to draw near: chachaddik, an approach: ma-achachaddik, activ. any one who comes near: activ. ma-achaddik, coming near. From machaddik, chaddik, the drawing near of a matter.

Chummad
42

好報、惡報

chinummad, chachúmmad, g. chadda, I. chadden, chinad, inochadden, retribution, whether good or bad; pachad, transit: chachad, reward: ma-achachad, a rewarder.

Chûmmaddip
42

拔/割掉接近地面的東西（？） （類似拔草、除草？農作物？）

chi, cha, chaddippa, to cut off any thing close to the ground.

Chummagchil
42

遇見正在走路、跑步的人

chinummagchil, chachummagchil, g. chachilla, I. chagchillan, chimagchillan, inochagchillan, to come up with any one in walking or running. Pachachil, chachûchchil, nom. subst. ma-achûchachil, a good runner that can overtake others.

Chûmmâi
43

背（動詞）

chinummai, chachûmmai, g. chai-a, *I. cha-in, chinai, inochaittin, to carry on the back. Pachai, transit: chachai, nomen. subst. ma-achachai;

Chummallak

Chûmmais
43

chi, cho, chaisa, pass. chaisas, a putting off. Pachais, transit.

Chummallûm
43

(v.)堆疊、使重疊 (n.)疊在一起的東西（？）如衣服

chinummallam, *chachummałlam, g. challama, any thing that lies over another, as clothes, &c. Also to hang or put one thing over another.

Chûmmalyal
43

狗吠聲

chi, cha, chalgalla, the barking of dogs. Pachalgal, transit. Chachalgal, gebas nom. ma-achchalgal, to bark.

*Chummannagh
43

在箭上刻凹痕，使其能固定成一串

chi, cha, *channagha, channaghan, chinannaghan, inochannaghan, to make a notch in an arrow in order to fix it on the string.

*Chummunied
43

（大人或小孩的） 尖叫聲、吼叫聲、哭喊聲

chinmumaniod, chachummanied, g. *channida, the screaming, howling, and crying, whether of children or adults.

Chûmmalt
44

付贖金給歹徒；付罰款；償還

chinûmmalt, chachûmmalt, g. chatta. I. chattan, chinattan, inochattan, to pay a ransom for a murderer: according to the old native custom, a pig for a man. Also to pay a fine for any misdeed. Pachalt, transit. to do as above: also simply to give back or repay one thing for another, like for like, whatever it be: chachalt, the punishment laid on any one a ransom for murderer. Also the judgment that is annexed to murder. Atea *zi_sja o chachalt o tapos o cho, the day of general judgment. Ma-achachalt, a ransomer; that is, one who pays the ransom.

*Chummappachappa
44

無恥的；自大的

chinummappachappa, chachûmmappachappa, g. chappachappa, stubborn, shameless, haughty; to hawl and tear in a quarrelsome manner: chiummaappachappo, cho, maibas, chammabal, chachappachappa, stubbornness; ma-achachappachappa, a stubborn, troublesome person.

Chümmacha
44

尋找

chinûmmacha, chachûmmûcha, chachachachûan, chinacha, inochachaas, to look for, to seek out. Pachacha, pi, pa, apachûcha, ipachacha, inipachacha, ino-ipachacha, to search out: piri mario. Chummacho o arribel, o naùpoot, to look out for good clothes: chummacho'mammal, to look out for a lover; it is used for men as well as things. Chachûcha, a searching out: maachachacha, to seek out.

Chummachcho
45

用鹼液洗

chinummachcho, chachûmmachcho, chachchoa, chachchoan, chinachchóau, inochachchoan, to wash with lye. Pachûchcho, pinachachcho, papachachcho, ipachachchoa, ipachachcho, inipachachcho, inoipachachcho, to do as above. Chummach cho-no riba, to wash clothes. Ma-achachachcho, a washerman. Chach-cho, lye to wash with.

Chûmmar
45

焚燒

chinûmmar, chachûmmûr, g. charra, I. charren, chinar, inocharren. inochûan, to burn up. Pachar, transit. Cho chummar aras baron, don charren; or chaan, chauman, people have set the grass on fire, and it is burnt; the fire consumes. Chúchar paga chûchar assaban, there is a fire in the village; ma-achachar, one who sets any thing on fire.

*Chummecheo
46

把洞弄大（？）

chinummeocheo, chachúmmeocheo, cheoche-óa, cheocheoon, chineocheoon, inocheocheoon, to bore a hold a little wider, as with a knife, the point of a bill, &c. Pacheocheo, pinacheocheo, papacheocheo, ipacheocheóa, ipacheocheo, inipûcheocheo, ino-ipacheocheo, to do as above.

Chummaraddo
46

環繞；包圍

chi. cha, charaddoa, charaddoon, chinaradodo, inocharadodoon, the same as rûmmarro, to encircle. Pacharûdodo, transit. chacharadodo. nom. chûmmarapo, chi, cha, charopoa, charapoon, chinarapo, inocharapoon, to cover a chamber with ant thing; to guard the window with a bamboo: chacharapo, from Pacharapo, a covering, or placing.

Chûmmarillochillo
46

Chûmmarop
46

chinummarop, chachûmmaróp, g. charoppa, l. charóppan, inicharop, inocharoppan, to gather amd take up with the hands, as rice, barley; also to rake dirt together. Pacharop, transit. from chacharop, such scraping together; ma-achacharop, to scrape anything.

Chûmmarrad

same as chûmmallam

Chûmmarod
47

穿襪子

chinummarrod, chachummarrod, g: charrodda, to put on one's stockings. Pacharrod, pi, pa, ipacharodda, &c. charroddas, chinarroddan, ino-charroddan; charroddan ja asiel, he legs are covered with stockings. Charrod, ipacharrod, the stockings are on. Charrod, stockings; ipacharrodoxia, put on the child's stockings.

Chûmmaschas
47

把東西刮平

chinûmmaschas, chachûmmaschas, g. chaschàssa, I. chaschassen, chinaschas, inochaschassen, to scrape any thing even.

Chümmat
47

漲潮

chinummat, chachûmmat, it is high water; but this is only said of the sea, and not of rivers. It is used when the water stands still, and does not flow. Châchat, high water. Sabunno ja chúmmat ai? When is it high water? Chûmmat ja to, it is high water.

Chummattad
47

遮蔽

chi, cha. chattûdda, chattaddan, chinattaddan. *inocha_taddan, to shadow, to over shadow. Pachattad, transit. nom. chattad. a shadowing. Chatta dan aijan, a shadowy place, a covering for the sun.

Chûmmaû
47

掃

chinûmmaû, chachûmmaû, g: chau-u, I. chaûan, *chiuaû, *inochaúnan, to sweep. Pachaû, transit. Chachaû; a besom: ma-achachaû, a sweeper: chochûmmaû, the man sweeps. Chauan ja don, the house is swept.

Chúmda
48

在季節初到時

chi, cha, cheda, chedûan, chienda, inochedûan, early in the season: as Padaat, Pachdo', transit. nom. chachda, early time.

Chûmme
48

chinumme, chachumme, g. chía, to do that which is suitable.

Chummeriel
48

鋸

chinummeriel, chachûmmeriel, to saw; cherila, cherilen, inocherilled. Pacheriel, pi, pa, ipûcherilla. a saw.

Chûmmero
48

拉直

chinûmmero, chachûmmero, g: chera, I. cheroan, chínero, inocheroon, to make straight. As Pachero, transit. chûmmero-noties, chache-ro, nom. sub. a making straight; also that by which any thing is made straight.

Chûmmi
48

用錐子戳洞

chinûmmi, chachûmmi, g. chia, I. chien, chini, inochieu, to bore a hole with a bodkin. Chaegi, a bore.

Chümmibur
48

攪拌食物（使不燒焦）； 划船

chinûmmibar, chûchûmmibar, g. chibarra. I. chibarren, chinibar, mochibarreo, to stir about food in the cooking, that it may not be burned. Also to row: Pachibar, chibûrren; inochan a bali, the food is well stirred; the boat is rowed. Chachibar, a stiring about: chachibar o abak, the rowing of a boat; ma-acha, chibar, a boatman, a rower.

Chümmichi
49 （頁面疑似有被切到）

倒入、倒出（液體）

chinummichi, chachûmmichi, g: ichichia, I: ichicha, inichicha, inochichi, to pour in, to cast in, as in a pot, can, or bottle, &c. to pour out. Pachichi, transit. from chumma. Otoichichi, the beer, wine, or water is poured out. Chûmmichi, oto o bonoaad_ maibas tûmmis, chachichi, a pouring out, or pouring in; chûche, chi oto, chamma, ma-achachichi, a cup bearer.

Chûmmied
49

（用籬笆等）圍住

chi, cha, chieddan, chidden, chinied, inochiëdden, to fence in, to inclose; Porchied. transit. Chached, a fence; ma-achachied, to inclose.

Chummieg
49

烤；炸

chinummieg, chachummieg, g. chiegcha, I: chiegchegen, chiniegch, inochiegchen, to roast; as summoso pachieg, chiegchen tsi biman, the fish or flesh is fried. Chachieg, a roasting, or frying; maachachien, a fry.

Chûmmillip
50

用矛刺、割

chinûmmillip, chachûmmillip, g: chilippa, I. chilippen, chinilip, inochinilippen, to cut with shears. Chummillip, naupoot, to cut linen; naupoot chilippen, the linen is cut up. Chachilip, scissars; ma-achachilip, one who cuts with scissars.

Chûmmimit
50

照顧、保護、統治

chinûmmimit, chachummimit, g: chimta, I. chimten, chinimit, inochimten, to secure, to take care of, to protect, to rule, to take charge of. Pachimit, transit. Ma-achachimt, a superintendent, a ruler. Chachimit, a rule. Pachimit, to take care of. Pachimit o assaban, a garrison to take care of a town.

the same as chûmmibar

Caûmmio
50

想辦法遠離他人

chinummio, chachummio, chiou, chioan, chinio, inochioan, chummio, no-man, michan patite, to do any thing when we do not want any one else near. Chûmmio no cho, to get away the people: cho chioan, the people are gone.

Chûmmior

樹發芽（？）

chinûmmior, chachûmmior. to sport forth as trees. Pachoir, transit. Gitas pûchior o barros, the rain makes the tress bud. Chioor, a bud.

Chûmmischis

摩擦竹子生火

chinummischis, chachummischis, g: chischissa, l: chischissea, chinischis, inochischissen, to produce fire by the rubbing of two bamboos together. Pûchischis, transitiv. Chûmmischis o chau: to produce fire.

Chûmmó

用藤蔓環裝飾

chinûmmio, chachummo, *choachoon, chino, ino-choon; Pacho, transit. to lace any thing with a string of rattan. Tairies choón o sarries chacho, a birding together: chachono tairies, a stringing of corals.

Chummoa

繫在一起

chinûmmoa, chachummonao, g. choa, I. choan, chinoa, inocho-an, to lace together. Pachoa, transit. Chachoa. a lacing together. *Chummoagagir, to lace the nets together, to fasten.

Chummime
51

擠出膿

chinummine, chachummime, chemea, cheme-in, chineme, ino-cheme-in, to press out pus from a *boil. Pûchemc, pinacheme, pûpûcheme, ipa-chemea, ipacheme. inipacheme, ino-ipacheme, to do as above. Chûmmime o soo, to press out a wound. Chemeis soa, the wound is pressed out. Cheme, pus.

Chumminoch

（因憤怒、輕蔑） 被丟棄、驅逐的人事物

chinumminoch, chachumminoch, chiuoch-a, chinoch-en, chininoch, inochinochen, that which is disapproved of in anger, or cast away in contempt Pachinoch, po, pa, ipachinocha, &c. to do as above. It betokens also to throw away any thing in anger and break it into pieces.

Chummir

如鳥般空中盤旋； （樹、草等）擺動

chi, cha, chirra, chirron, chinir, inochirran, to hover as birds when they keep their wings still. Pachier, to do as above. It is used also of trees or grass, when they gently wave their heads.

Chûmmisel

畫直線(right line)

chirrlchen, chinirrich, inochirrichen, to draw a tight line. Pachirrich, pi, pa, ipachirricha, ipachirrich, inipachirrich, ino-ipachirrich, to do as above. Chûmmirrich, as kûmmirrich, chachirrich, a right line.

Chummoar
52

the same as chûmmibar

Chummomach

chinummomach, cha-chummomach, chomûcha, chomachen, chinomach, inccho-machen, to rule. Chummomach o sassi, to salt. Fachomach, pipapa chomach, ipachomach-a, ipachomach, inipachomach, ino-ipa chomach, to do as above. Chummomach o abo, to plaster with lime.

Chummo-a-cho

Chummo-acho-ar

chinummo-acho-ar, chachummo-acho-ar, g: cho-acho-arra, I: cho-acho-arren, chino-acho-ar, inocho-acho-arren, to mix one thing with another; to stir up from the bottom, as chummibar. Pacho acho-ar, transit.

Chûmmobbechob

捲起袖子；打起精神努力

chinummobbechob, chachûmmobbechob, g: chobbechobba, I: chobbechobben, chinobbechob, ino-chobbechobben, to tuck up, to strip up, as the sleeves of a coat. Also to stir up to diligence in work. Pachobechoob, transit: chachobechoob, nomen. Chummobechoob o tummaap, to stir up. Cho, chobechoben, chûmmobechoob, riba, lili, o liba, the clothes or sleeves stripped up.

Chummobon
53

放進（刀劍等的）鞘

chinûmmobon, chachûmmobon, g. echoboma, I. ichobon, inichobon, ino-chiobon, to put into the sheath, the sheath. Chobonnan, chinobonnan, inochobonnan. Pachobon, transit. Chobon, nomen. a sheath.

Chûmmod

通姦；尋求不當（男女）關係

chinummod, chachûmmod, g: chodda, I: chodden, chinod, inochodden, to commit adultery, to seek an improper connection: or the improper connection itself. Sai sini, sù chummod ina, mirab palro achachoa, sjiem, ____ is a woman come to ask me to ______ her son go free. Pachod, transit. Chachod, whoredom, adultery. Ma-achachad, a whoremonger, an adultery.

Chûmmollichol

to put out, to put away

chinummollichol, chachûmmollichol, g: chollicholla, I: chollichollen, chinollichol, inochollichollen, to put out, to put away. Pachollichol, transit. Chachollichol, nomen.

Chû mmolliet

the same as hûmmahimmotto

chi, cha, chollietta, chollietten, inocholliën, inocholliëtten, the same as hûmmahimmotto; chachollien, nom. chûmmollicholp riba, to undress. Chûmmollichol o bazigh, villen.

Chûmmollok

用同種類的物品取代

chinûmmollok, chachummollok, g: chollokka, I: chollokkan, chinollokkan, inochollokkan, to change things of the same sot one with another, whether openly or in secret. Pachollok, transit. Chachollok, to exchange, barter, chachollok o arribil.

Chummonagh
54

引起（不好的、邪惡的事）

chi, cha, chinagha, chonaghen, chinonagh, ino-chonûghen, as lummalla. Pachonagh, as lalala. Ma-achàchonag, als ma-alalala.

Chummoschos

粗糙地剪/砍下來的東西

chinûmmoschos, chachummoschos, g: choschossa, I: choschossen, chinoschas inochoschossen, anything badly, or raggedly cut.

Chûmmonchos

犁，耕

chi, cha, chonchonna, plough. Chachonchon, a ploughing.

Chummo-o

從地上長出

chinummo-o, chachûmmo-o, to spring out of the ground. Pacho-o, pi, pa, ipachooa, ipacho-o, inipacho-o ino-ipacho-o, to arise, to spring up. Cho-o, a sprout.

Chûmmomochomo

用手掌摩擦、磨蹭

chinummomochomo, chachummomochómo, chomochómoa, chomochomoon, chinomochomoon, inochomochomoon, to rub anything gently with the palm of the hand. Pachomochomo, to rub with the hand the place that itches.

Chûmmoschos

????????

chi, cha, choschosse, pass. choschossen. chinoschos, inochoschossen, idem tùmmachos. Pachoschos, transit.

Chummoté

處罰

chinummoté, chachummote, choten, chote, chinoté, inochoten, to punish; as tummea, and pachote; chachoté, punishment. Ma-achachote, punishing.

Chummottol

一拳

a blow with a fist.

Chumpe

扁平像板子的竹子

chinumpe, chachumpe, g: chuppea, I: chuppein, chinuppe, ino-chuppein, bamboos make flat like boards. Pachuppe, transit.

Chumpir

穿過（草叢、水面、敵人等）

chinumpir, chachumpir, chuppirra, chuppirren, chienpier, ino-chûppirren, to break through; as men say, chunopir o arros, o to, o azijes, to push through the grass, the water, the enemy, &c. Pachûppir, pinachuppir, papachuppir, ipachûppirra, to do as above. Chachuppir, a breaking through; chachuppir o to, the braking through of water.

Chumpod

(水)從地底冒出來

chinumpod, chachumpod, to spring out of the ground, as water.

Chumrar

芽從根部冒出

chi, cha, the shooting forth of many sprouts from the root.

Chumsan
56

吸/吐氣

chinumsan, chachûmsan, the in- and expiration of the breath. It differes from paucher, which means to blow strongly; chachsas, nom. the breath.

Chuppé

弄平了的竹子

a flttened piece of bamboo. From chumpé.

Chuppin

狼

the woof. Chuppin o naupoot.

Chúppod

泉；井

a well, a fountain. From chumpod.

Da

死亡、乾和（是字根？）

an aflix, as macha-da, dead, dry; ma-bada, wize, to know.

Daal

稻草(種子被取出來之後)

a straw; after the seed is threshed out.

Daddalizi

一種舞蹈

a dance, from dûmmalizi.

Daddassas

鳥的嗉囊

the crop of birds.

Dagh

終結；過去

over, done: ka dagh ja zichil, the sorrow is over: ka dagh ja mapich, the fight is done: ka dagh ja oba, the drowsiness is past.

Dachûm

雲的陰影

the shadow or darkness which the clouds make on the ground, when they obscure the sun; for otherwise the shdow of a tree is called eonno. Verbum, midach-um. Paidach-um, transit.

Dadach

(植物的)莖

the stalk of plants, melons, &c.

Dakrap
57

存在、坐（？？？）

cannot well be trasnlated(???): dakrap ja mampa, there sits the bird: innai bonna da mai dakrap, I am come out of the field, and here I sit.

Dallassan o bam

時鐘

Darri dûrri, a clock.

Dalli

鶺鴒（一種鳥）

the wagtail. Hence the proverb. tumcha inasoan, sai don ja dalli, mameroos jà badda, masumak ja baas, the northern monsoon approaches; the swallow returns to her house; the bachelors wish to marry; it is now the time for pairing.

Datta

河岸

the bank of a river; written dûtta: lallûbbo, lobbokas, the sea shore.

Daûkirrap

一種鼻笛

a double flute on which people plat with their nostrils.

Daûtatsitlichen

小指

the little finger.

Dûzino

在飛的風箏

a flying kite: as taz-i.

Dazjo

(劍、刀的)刀面

the blade of a sword or knife, to which the handle is fixed.

De
58

在某處；靠近某處

in, somewhere, there: de don, in the house: de Tackais, near Tackais: but the de is commonly joined to two other words, as lellum, and pana, of which the first means in, and the second there; thus instead of the above, they say, de lellum don, pana de Tackais: de is not seldom found after innai, and thus serves to point out a place; as innai de errenerren, from Favorlang; de means also near, paga barron de tabaipaû ja don. Nataroa, mini, de lellum, inni, is of the same meaning: sometimes i is used, as kakoren i barrien, for lellum.

Decho

他們

they.

Deeg/Dillij

報應

any evil that we deserve, or have brought on ourselves; thus they say, jo a deeg, or dillij, it is well arranged, you have your deserts.

Dema

疑問詞（誰、什麼、哪一個、哪裏）

who, what, which, where.

Dema

哪裏

indema, indea, inde, de, are all of one meaning, as pana dema, pana de, where are you going? N. B. Nûmma is sometimes used for dema, as mosse-numma, for mosse-dema.

Dipa

以免

lest.

Dich

一種疾病

a sickness. From Madich.

Dille

幼鳥

all sorts of yound birds, just hatched and not yet fledged.

Dimmo

往上拉

zinemmo, dadimmo, g. doa, I: doon, zinoon, inodoon, to pull upwards, to hoist, as people draw water out of a well. Pado, transit. Dummono dale, to. draw up a pitcher: dale kadoon, means also to take a pot off the fire.

Dippi

鐵

iron.

Doat

長滿蘆葦的叢林

a jungle full of reeds and rushes, such as grow on the banks of rivers and morasses.

Dogh
59

禮儀；傳統

manner, custom: kadogh, constume, ceremonies: kadóg o assaban, kadog o anibaas, maibas madarrain.

Don
60

房子；大船

a house, a great vessel.

Doogh
60

my head beats(???)

to beat: ka doogh ja na öeno, my head beats; as tummok. Doogh has no tenses.

Dorren
60

嘴唇

the lips

Dummarau
60

折彎成半圓形

zinûmmaraû, tadûmmaraû, g. daraû-a, I. daraûn, zenaraû,inodaraun, to bend half round, to make a semi-circle. Padaraû, transit. modaraû, semi-circular: neutr. daddaraû, a semi-circle.

Dummadach
60

爬

dsi, tad: dadacha; dadachen, &c. to climb. Padadach, transit.

Dûmmadach
60

（使）成為圓

to make into a circle; imp: daraûdaûn.

Dûmmaribodibo
60

像一個圓

the same; imp. taribodiboa, modaaraûdaû, modaribodibo, like a circle; daddaraûdaû, daddaribodibo, a circle.

Dûmmaries
60

上鎖

zinummaries, tadummarries, g: darriesa, I: idarries, inidarris, inoidarries, darriessan, inidarries, darriessan, to lock up, or fasten. Padarries, transit. chachap idarries, don darriessan: dandarries, a lock.

Dûmmarrogigodoggo
60

瘸腿走路（？？）

zinummarrogigodoggo, tadûmmarogodoggo, g. darroggodoggo-a, to walk double, as old people or those who are deformed do, to spy out anything. Maibas kakkollen. pikkon sies: daddarroggodoggo, nom. as ababad pikkon, a hunch back.

Dûmmaû
61

替代、取代

to do anything in the place of another, or to succeed to one, dsi, tadum: imp. daua: nomen dau, instead of another. Maanaû, one who comes in the place of another to do or suffer anything for them.

Dûmmaûko
61

抬頭

zinûmmaûko. tadúmmaûko, g. daûkóa, to lift up the head high, either because people can see with difficulty, as mitébabo baak, or that they do it, inomaso kummeriel, to pay the more attention.

Dummo-an
61

流汗

zinûmmo-an, inodùmmoan, to sweat. Dûmmoan ja ina, I sweat. Dûmmo, sweat.

Dùmmaûkaûka
61

醉漢蹣跚而行

zinûmmaûkàûka, tadûmmaûkaûka, g: daûkaûka-a, is said of drunkards who go staggering about the streets.

Dûmmeódeo
61

長、飄逸

zinûmméódeo, tadûmmeódeo, long and trailing, as a long garment, a long tail, long hair, &c. Dûmeódeo, arriba, taa, the gown trails, the hair hangs long.

Dùmmeogh
62

刷；磨擦

zinûmmeogh, tadûmmeogh, g: déogcha, I. deógchen, zineogh, inodeogchen, to brush, or rub off. Dûmmeógo o sesnab, to brush down with a brush: dûmmeog o rima. to rub down with the band. Padeoch, transit. taddeoch, nomen. subst. Dûmmeogh o magcha, to rub the eyes: dûmmeogh o nok, to blow the nose.

Dúmbor
62

強行奪走、搶走

zinumbor, tadûmbor, doborra, doborren, zinobor, inodoborren, padabor, transit. to take away against one's will: as maûpis, poas: ka sai dumbor na mochan ja mado, the dog has taken away my food; to constrain another to do any thing, either willingly or not; to hold fast, and not to left go: as madabdab, elli pittol o meacha, dombor o maùmali o meroos. Dûmbor o arribil, dûmbor o cho, to force any one, to take any thing away: nomen. subst. daddobor, daddobor o ballag, depriving another of his goods. Ma addobor, an oppressor, a tyrant.

Dummaat
62

接近，靠近

zinummaat, tadûmmaat, g: daatta, to approach, to draw near. Passi. daatten, dsinaat, inodaatten, that which is approached. Padaat, to draw near; dûmmadaat, intend. taddaat, a drawing near; dûmmaat o assaban o sabba, dûmmaat ta deon.

Dummachal
63

（用鋤頭等）翻地

dsi: tad. dach-alla, dachûllen, zinach-al, ino-dach-allen, to turn over the over the ground with a spade or hoe. Padach-al, daddach-al, a digging up, also a hoe. Ma ataddach-al, a digger.

Dummaggo
63

（樹木、房屋、人）站不直

zinummaggo, tadûmmaggo, imp. daggo-a, not to stand upright, to over hang; is generally said of men, houses, trees, &c. padaggo, transit. Dummaggo, o moddan asjoddon, the gable or wall hangs over. Tadaggo, nomen. subst.

Dummakkal
63

緞帶、繃帶

dsi, tad, see tûmmakkal, to bind. Daddakkal, a ribbon, a bandage.

Dummallap
63

用茅草蓋屋頂

dsi: tadum: dalappa, to thatch a house with grass. that is when a portion of the old thatch remains.

Dummalimogh
63

天空起霧、變得模糊

h, zinûmmalimogh, tadûmmalimogh, is said of the sky, when it appears hazy as in a drizzling shower. Dûmmalimogh o busûm.

Dummalizi
63

跳舞

zi, tad, dalizia, dalizian, zinalizau, inodalizian, to dance. Padalizi, transit. daddalizi, a dance. Maadaddalizi, a dancer.

Dummap
64

追上，趕上

zinûmmap, tadûmmàp, dappa, dappen, zinap, inodappen, as chûmmachil.

Dummarraab
64

使有線條；排齊；偷情

zinùmmarrab, tadûmmarrab, g: darrabba, I: darraban, zinarraban, ino darranban, to line, or to fix the lining in a garment. Also to put one garment over another. Also to live in aultery. Padarrab, transit.

Dummarradarrab
64

Dummarraab的負數

the plural of the preceding. Padarrab, transitiv. Hence dardarab, lining.

Dûmmapal
64

撞到

zinummalpal, tadûmmapal, g. dapûlla, I. dapallan: dapallan baron, baro asiel, rima oenoete idapal, idapal, inidapal, inoidapal, zinapallan, inodapallan, to run against any thing, as kadoog; padapal, transit. daddapal, apush, a clash: daddapal o asiel.

Dûmmarram
64

（在學習的過程中）實作

zinúmmarram, tadûmmarram, g: darrama, to practice one's self in any thing, is used both for teacher and learner. Passi. darramen, dsimarran, inodarranmmen, dummarran, tûmmoch o bido, to practice one's self in reading; is verbum act: dûmmarram o sisjien o tûmmoch o bido, the children exercise themselves in reading. Madarram, as maba. Padarram, dûminarram, acho maba. Dûmmarram meach ta Deos, to practice one's self, or to learn to pray. Daddaram, nom. exercise. Daram, to exercise one's self, nom. exercise. Taddaram, one who is practised. Daddarran o aiacha,a meeting for prayer. Ma adaddarram, one who exercises himself or another.

Dûmmaraggadaggal
65

跌倒

zìnûmmaraggadaggal, tadûmmaraggadaggal, darraggadaggalla, to stumble.

Dûmmirdir
65

蹲下，坐下

dsi, tad, imp. dasdissen, to sit, to squat down, as when men sit on their heels. Padasdis, transit. nom. daddasdis.

Dûmmittia
65

半途停下

zinûminittin, tadûmmittin, g. dittina, to stop half way, not to go out.

Dûmmoas
65

（酒）不夠陳

dsi, tad, doassa, doassen, dsinoas, inodoassen, is said of liquor when it is too fresh, that people may make it more sour or more sweet. Padoas, transit. daddoas, dummoas machoch, put some more acid in it: daddoas. make it sweeter.

Dummobdob

叫醒別人

tsi, ta, dobdobba, dobdobben, dsinobdob, ma dobdobben, to wake up any one. Padobdob, transit. Sadobdob, nom. Ma addobdob, one who wakes up another.

Dummochol

用拳頭打胸口

zinûmmochol, tadûmmochol, docholla, dochollen, zinochol, ino dochollen, to strike with the fist on the breast. dadochol, nom.

Dûmmoelallis

dsi, tad, didossa, pass. dosdossen, &c. ja to, to tap, or let off liquor. Padodos, transit

Dummoragh

（不使人受傷地）輕打別人

zinûmmoelallis, tadûmmoelallis, g: doelalissa, I: doelalissen, zinoelallis, inodoelallissen, to hit people slightly, without hurting them.

Dummorab

剝皮（？？）

zi, ta, g: doragcha, I: to flay, chûmmorach, idem.

Dummorat

放鬆

zinûmmorat, tadûmmorat, g. doratta, I. doratten, zinorat, inodoratten, to relieve. Chûmmorat, idem. Padorat, transit. dadorat, nom.

Dummori

否認；拒絕

zinûmmori, tadûmmori, g: dorria, to deny, to speak against.

Dummoro

走入

(the last o sounded short) zinummoro, tadûmmoro, g: dorro, to go in. Contract, dorro, dsinorro, &c. daddoro, nom.

Dummorsdos

拖著腳走路

dsi, tad, dosdossa, passi. dosdossen, &c. ja ta, to trail one feet. Padosdos, transit.

Dumpûl
鞥‘

放火

zi, ta, dûppûlla, dûppûllen, dsinûmpûl. inodûppûllen, to set on fire. Paduppul, transit.

Dudûppûl

縱火罪

nom. arson. Ma adûddûpûl, one who sets on fire..

Eeb

柴火

fire wood.

E-è

草地、蜂蜜和水（奶與蜜之地？？）

mead, honey and water.

Eicham-an

用來喝東西的工具

anything to drink out from. From micham, to drink.

Eichaman

煙斗

chatto, a tabacco pipe.

Elli

用於否定（類似否定詞）

to deny, as with us, no: but it is only used in connection with another word: as elli mabisse oaseis. your heart is not true. Elli pa, is so common that nothing can exceed it. and yet i do not know that is the real meaning of it (then what about me?????). It seems to signify that some thing is not in existence, as elli pa ja adda de assaban o amicien: or that some thing is not in one possession; as ellipa ja oa bido ina-ai, the first of which I cannot otherwise understand than that "there is no rice in the village on the north:" and the other "I have not got your book." See in alli.

Erab

唾沫

spittle.

Eran

一種小豆子

certain small beans.

Erien

臀部

the hip.

Erotorûtto

蟾蜍

a toad.

Gaat

尖端

a point. From Maggaat. Gûmmaat, gi: ga: gata: gatan: ginaat, to sharpen, to bring any thing to a point. to carve. Ginaat, cut. Gagaat, a sharpening. Ma-agagaat, to sharpen. Ma-aggaat, a sharpener.

Gagoor

陽具

the penis.

Gemnea

打嗝

gi, ga, gea, to belch, to eructate. Pagea, transit. nom: gagea, a belching.

Giacho

water mixed with herbs, with which the women wash the houses.

Giroan

一半

half.

Giech

扯開東西

a word that is used when any thing tears.

Goeng

Gomila

Gorrogot

鴿子

a dove. Don o gorrogot, dove cot.

Gummabgab

割草，割小米

gi, ga, gabgabba, the cutting of paddy, or millet. Rûmmabies, idem. Pagabgab, transit.

Gummachhach

gi, ga, gachhacha, pass, gachhachen, &c. Pagachhach, transit. to hoe away the ground from a house in a sloping direction. Gagachhach, nom.

Gummigidsi

觸發

gi, ga, gagidsia, to tickle active. pagagiesi, transit. Gagidsi, a tickling. Maagagidsi, a tickler.

Gummaggri

gummagissi是什麼⋯⋯

Gumma-iech

Gummatach

切割（樹木、水果等）

gi, ga, gatacha, gatachen, ginatach, inogatachen, pagatach, transit. gatach, nom. to split up large pieces of wood; but when bamboos are spoken of, pilla is used. It is also used in the cutting up of pumpkins, melons, plantains, &c.

Gummeoch

用茅草蓋屋頂

gi, ga, geocha, to thatch house.

Gummesar

腸絞痛；一把；麻煩事 （？？？？）

(let the (e) be scarcely heard) gi, ga, gesarra, gesarran, the same as gummiddiggit: gesar, just as if people said gsar, a gripe, a handfull.

Gummeach

築籬笆；防禦

gi, ga, giacho, giachen, giniach, ino-giachen, to fence, or secure; people say also, giûchen ja sabba, as if the river were suddenly swollen and therefore a fence was made. Pagiach, transit. nom. gigiach, a fence.

Gummiach

伸懶腰

gi, ga, giacha, giachen, giniach, inogiachen, to stretch out the arms, as lazy people do; as paggeas, merely, to reach out the arm, leg, finger, &c. neutr. magiach.

Gummiddiggit

握拳；快速抓住物品

gi, ga, giddiggitta, giddiggitten, ginigddiggit, ino-giddiggitten, to close the hand. Also to grasp any thing fast. nom. gagiddiggit, a fist.

Gumnab

開始

gi, ga, gnabba, gnabben, ginab, ino-gnabben, to begin. As ptat, and pto. Gagnab, nom. as paptat.

Gummo

小

small.

Gûmmoch

合併

gi, ga, gocha, gochen, ginoch, ino-goch, pagoch, transit. Gagoch, nom: to bind together.

Gummamgan
71

the same as gûmmoch

Gummomach
71

gi, ga, gomacha, gomachen, ginummach, inogomachen, to rub out any thing that is drawn or written. Pagomach, transit. gûgomach, nom.

Hoadsi

Herien

Ja
71

a particle denoting interrogation, ja madûrram jonoe ta Deos o Baûsie, do you know the God of the Dutch?

Jenmanat

Jes

Ibien
71-72

本義：蛇 *ibien ota: 小紅蛇 ibien o aras: 斑紋蛇 ibien abo: 寛腹蛇 ibien baron or isaijs: 硬脊蛇 ibien marali: （可能是）眼鏡蛇 ibien e ribij: 蛇匍匐而入穀倉 *ibien o atei: 蛇鼓起口腔（？） *ibien o boesûm korrokorron maûsi: 黑白相間的蛇（雨傘節） *ibien tagotago de abas, korrokorroan mekach maûsi, mali kach ja ki-or: 海蛇（有綠白色斑紋、寬尾） (*打星號表示蛇很毒XD)

a snake. *ibien ota, small red snake, makaka. ibien o aras, korrokorroan, a spotted snake. ibien abo, a large bellied snake, matoatsi. ibien baron or isaijs, a snake hard in the back, mattilo, maraas asieg ibien marali, a snake with large eyes, matoto macha. ibien e ribij, snakes that creep quietly along the ground, and remain in the granaries. *ibien o atei, a snake that blows its cheeks up: mato a ri. *ibien o boesûm korrokorron maûsi, snakes spotted with black and white. *ibien tagotago de abas, korrokorroan mekach maûsi, mali kach ja ki-or, snakes found in the sea. spotted green and white with broad tails.

Ichien
72

鸚嘴鉤

a hook, like a parrot's bill.

Icho

he

Idas

Idod

Idorrodorrûs
72

一種鼠類（fan？）

Iel-iel

桑葚；Baron o iel-iel 桑葚樹； Bo' o iel-iel 桑葚果

Iem-dan

灼熱的小疹子

Ikkil

Imigh-igh
72

inimigh-igh, amigh-igh, g: igh-igha: l: igh-ighen, migh-igh, inoigh-ighen, to gnaw, to nibble. Imighigh o ûso, to bite the nails.

Karri of mau,
77

為該族的習俗。 語其他部落的居民訂定和平契約時，會扯下對方衣服上的一根草吃掉。 此舉為和平的象徵。

aan a tammas, or harri or man, aan, o rarozì, is the manner of the natives. when they will make a treaty of peace with each other; they pluck a thread out of each other's clothes and eat it up; which is a sign of peace: this contract is made midway between their villages.

mi, machanacha, nertr.? notched. See chûmmanach. Chanag, a notch in an arrow.

Machapor

Machi-ag chi erab

胡說

mi, ma to drivel: achi achi erab, or machi achi, mi, ma, achi a chia, this is also to leak; nom. achi a ch, and achi a chi erab, slaver. Ma achi achi, one who drivels. Pachia chi erab, and pachi a chi, transi. Ma chiagchi, composed from machiagchi, to leak, and erab, spittle. Machiagchi ohallaonan, the pot leaks. Achiagchi in, inachiagchi in, ina achisgchi in ja to, the water is leaked out.

Madallolees
114

發亮的

mi, ma, neutr. glistering, shinning, as if well scoured: but this only refers to any thing that has a white ground, and differs from raosan.Dallolees, nom. a shining, it is also the name of a tree, the bark of which shines like the European beech.

Madodevbo-ibo
116

Magaiech

Magak
117

Magchitagchitat
117

未決定的、可改變的

mi, ma, unsettled, changeable: mi, ma, agchitagchitatta, is not said of men's will or words, but refers to things that exist now and then, as magchitagchitat moetas, it rains some times. Agchitagchitat, changeableness.

Magga
117

達成目標的手段

minagga, mamagga, agga, the means in order to an end, yaga, miagga, inojagga, the object or aim; agan, inagan, inoaggan, to throw out of the hand. Maggo taggargar, to cast anchor. Paga, trans. Aga, the throwing of projectiles. Ma aga, one skilful in throwing.

Maggo-aan
117

投擲

Maggo-aan, mi, ma, aggo-ana, compounded of magga, to throw, and ann, food; when tow parties, after having promised their children, previous to the marriage, feed each other. Paggo-an, trans. aggo-aan, nomen. subst.

Maggaat
117

被指向的

mi, ma, sharp: agaata, pointed. Maggaat o zinoe, a sharp knife: maggaato raro, a three cornered hat. Maggagaat, intend. from gummaat. Gaat, a point. Ma agaat, any thing pointed.

Magge
118

堅韌的、黏的

mi, ma, imp. aggea, tough, sticky, paste made from rice, starch, &c.

Maggogh
118

惹腦

mi, ma, aggocha, to annoy by vexation. Maggogh ja na, azijel o mababat, maggoghja, maggogh ja na babiaro machip. Pagoch, trans. goch, vexation. Ma agoch, vexer. Pagoch, act. agocha, &c. trans. ipagocho, &c.

Maggos
118

用網抓魚

mi, ma. agossa, to fish with a sweep net, bu which the fishes are inclosed. Pagos, transi.

Maggotarrar
118

彎曲某物

mi, ma to bend any thing on the edge or end, as the edge of a napkin, &c. Also to go slanting upwards, as a way. Pagotarrar, trans. et act. imp. agotarrarra, agotarrarran, ipagotarrarra, pas. ipagotarrar, &c.

Magoûlyk
118

扭到腳

Magoûlyk, mi, ma, agoulyka, neutr. to sprain the foot, to wrench. Pagoûlyck, act. et trans. a sprain of the foot. The natives cure this by the leaves of a certain tree, called satik, with which they bind up the limb in order to soften the skin, or to disperse the extravasated blood.

Magomach
118

消失

mi, ma, agomacha, neutr. blotted out. See gûmmach.

Magoragh
119

擦去的皮

mi, ma, agoracha, the skin rubbed off; magoragh ja rima, the skin is off my hand. Magar aggorach, intend.

Mai
119

來

mimai, mamai, imp. moa, to come. the 3rd person has sai, sanai, sasai, trans. only in the 3rd person, pasai, pi, pa: ipasaya. Mai, is he well? interrogatively.

Mai-acho
119

與我們有關的人 (親戚)

Mai-acho, all those who are related to us, whether male or female; also step father and mother. Seems to be compounded from the verbs Mai, to come, and macho, to bring; because when the daughters marry, they bring their husbands home to dwell.

Maibas
119

相似物

alike: mi, ma, imp. aubasa, aibas, nom. likeness. Ma aibas, one who makes alike. Paibas act. et trans. imp. aibasa, aibasan, inaibasan, inoaibasan, ipaibasa, ipaibas, &.

Maibat
119

為另一人工作

minaibat; mamaibat, aibadda, aibaddan, inaibaddan, ino-aibaddon, to work for another for one's board. as the poor do for a meal. Men say also mikat. Paibar, trans. with respect to the person who is served; aibat, nom. service. Maibat, a servant, a labourer. Pas. aibadden, inaibda, inaibadden, inaibad, inoaibadden, with respect to the hire that is obtained.

Majed
120

小的、好的

mi, ma, small, fine; but it is only said of many, for with regard to few it is keuzi; also than not thick. As makied. Paied, to make small. Ma-a-ied, or makikied, thin, Pa-i-ied, pakikied, trans.

Ma-allas
120

冷靜

Ma-allas, calm, cleared up; is said of wind and weather, also of the feelings. Pa-allas, act. et trans. imp. a-allassa, a-allassen, ina-allassen, ino-a-allassen, ipallassen, ina-allassen, ino-a-allassen, ipallassa. &c. Allas, nom. calmness, clearness. Ma-a-allas, a soother.

Ma-im-it
120

意圖

Ma-im-it, makiki, idem. Me-imimit, intend. makilikili, idem. middling, not too much, passable, neither too large nor too small. Is also used as machapor, and machapochapor, and then means moderate in conversation, neigher too still, nor too talkative.

Mairo
120

改變

kagmairo, mi, ma, aiman, airoan, airoa, inairoan, ino airoan, to change; as men do the teeth, or bucks the horus. Pairo, trans. nom. airo, a changing. Ma-airo, a changer.

Mais
120

minais, mamais, assa, aisan, inaisaa, inoaisan, to laugh. Pais, transais, a laugh. Ma-ais, a laugher.

Ma-issal
121

Ma-issal, mina-issal mama-issal, a-is-salla, to repeat, as children do before their master. Ma-issal o bido, to say out of book. Ma-issal o sies, to say by heart.

Maizi
121

接近

mi, ma, aizia, near, at hand: people say also maizi, aizi, and arri, neighbourhood. Aizi, paizi, act. and trans. amp. aizia, aizian, inaizi, inoaizian, ipaizia, pas. ipaizi, inoipaize. Maaizi, nom. and ma arzi, one who brings near.

Makabol
121

Megogach
121

minagagach, mamagagagh, agagagcha, to itch after, to desire strongly. Magagagagach, intend. magagach. Pagagach, trans. gagach, an itching, a disire. Ma-agagach, one who itches.

Ma-kairi
121

Ma-kairi, mi, ma, to do any thing with the left hand; as makairi ja simioch, pattite, &c. Ma annigh, idem. Ma akairi, a left handed man.

Ma-kallamas
122

Ma-kallamas, mi, ma, to do any thig with the right hand; as makallamas ja simioch, pattite, &c. Ma allamas, do.

Makakan

Makinkin

Makkas

ma, mi, akkassa, akkassen, inakkas, inoakkassen, to revile any one, to accuse, to reproach. Pakkas, trans. Makkas o ma atattosik, to accuse falsely. Akkas, a reviling. Maakkas, a reviler.

Makkeshap

吃壞肚子的聲音

the squeamishness of the stomach after having eaten any thing nauseous. mi, ma, marossoal ja ma-achaan inai o micbam.

Marotûl
143-144

一無所有；不再有

without any thing, deprived of everything. Ta Deos marotul ja bog, God is incorporeal, i.e. without a body, *pr. iut. ma, nom. deprivation, see the root rummûtul. Ma-arotul, one who is destitute. The Favorlang people do not use this word thus, but as the end of a chair, or table; still it comes to the same thing, for where any thing ends. there it exists no more.

Matincho
155

臃腫的；水腫的

minatincho, is said of the sea water, when it stands still between ebb and flood, because the sea then appears swollen. It is also said of the belly, when men are full, or when belly swells. It betokens also a little putrid, because when any thing begins to stink it swells up.

Maûchil
p158

完成的

Maûchil, mi, ma, aûchilla, neutr. accomplished, as machult. Pauchil, to accomplish, trans. et act, imp. ipauchilla, auchillen, inaûchil, inoaughillen, auchilla, pas. ipauchil, &c. Aûchal, a consummation; ma-auchil, a finisher.

Maúcho
p159

討厭的

Maû kar motto
p159

Maû kar motto, chacholliet, mi, ma, the same as maû-sasaki motto.

Maûchûs
p159

非常

Maûchûs, very, mi, ma, achûssa; maû-chus madich, very sick, perhaps also too sick, as mauchus mazilo, too long, also bold courageous, maûchûs, o aga, skillful with missile weapons; maûchus o babido, clever at the pen. Aûchusso,aûchussen inaûchûs,inoauchussen,imp. ipaûchussa, pass. ipauchussen, or auchussan, with respect to the instrument with which any thing is done. Pauchus,trans. et act. butokens any thing consummated, also leaving off; means also to dart across, or run through. Aûchûs,completeness, used also adverbially; maaûchûs, an accomplisher.

Maûdûm
p159

黑暗的（可用於心理上）

Maûdûm, dark, applied also to the mind, mi, ma, aûdûmma. Paûdûm, trans. odûm, darkness; ma-odûm, a darkener.

Maûkat
p159

愛，使...高興

Maûkat, minaûkat, mamaûkat, aûkatta,aûkattan, inaûkattan, inoaûkattan, to love, to rejoyce. Paûkat, trans. aûkat, love, joy; ma-aukat, a lover.

Maûkatir
p159

Maûkatir, mi, ma, aûkatirra, &c. as madûddo. Paûkatir, trans. nom. katir.

Maûnionis
p160

特別的

Maûnionis, mi, ma, aûnionisa, aûnionisen,inaunionis, inoaunionissen, intend. inaûnis, especial. Paunionis, trans. nom. _aûnionis, particularity, peculiar property.

Maûnisso arûch
p160

獲得或繼承某物以適合自己

Maûnisso arûch, minaûnisso arach, mamaûnisso arach, aûnisso arach-a, aûnisso arach-en, &c. toappropriate to one's self, by taking possession or inheriting of another'sgoods. Paûnisso-arach, trans. Aûnisso-arach, nom. ma-aunisso-arach, an heir.

Maûnis
p160

私人的

Maûnis, mi, ma, aûnisa,pricate, not common, se maûnis patodon, he is gone to reside at his own place. Paûnis, act. et trans. imp. aûnisa, aûnisaa, inaûnissen, inoaûnissen, ipaunisa, pas. ipaûnis, &c. Aunis, property; maaûnis, proprietor; maûnis o ala, mi, ma, imp. aûnis o ala, to speak to particularly, to testify.

Maûpi
p160

小或細的事物

Maûpi, minaupi, mamaûpi, any thing beaten small or fine. See paûpi; ma-aupi, a beater.

Maûpies
p160

努力去做某事

Maûpies, minaupies,mamaupis,aupisû, aûpisan, inaûpisan, inoaupisan, to strive about any thing, to scramble. Paûpies, trans. aûpies, a scrambling; ma-aupies, a scrambler.

Maûpulla
p161

以任何手段尋求、獲得或提升

Maûpulla, mi, ma, aûpûlla, to seek gain or advantage by any means. Aûpûl-, la, nom. a seeking of gain: ma-aû-pûlla, a gain seeker.

Maûranies
p161

玩，開玩笑

Maûranies, minaûranies, mamaûranies, aûranisa, auranisen, &c. to play; to joke. Pauranies, trans. Auranies, play; ma-auranies, a jester.

Mauroman
p161

打算

Mauroman, and mauroma-roman, intend. mi, ma, imp. auromanomama, to differ, to vary. Pauroma-roman, pi, pa, act. et trans. to make different. Auroman, nom. difference.

Mausa
p161

指野草都被燒光或是清理乾净的區域

Mausa, mi, ma, is said of a field when the weeds are burned down, or other wise cleared away. Pausa, pi, pa, osaá, pass. osa-an, inosa-an, ino-osaan. Osa, nom, a clearing away; from posa; ma-aosa, one who clears away. Ausa, clearness, from mausa.

Mau-sasakimotto
p161

橫向的

Mau-sasakimotto, mi, ma, transverse. Compounded from mau, and sasakimotto.

Mausi
p161

白色

Mausi, white, mi, ma, ausia. Pausi, trans, Osi, whiteness; ma-aosi, white, as ma-ausi.

Mautatarroggi
p161

通過欺詐手段換取他人貨物

Mautatarroggi, changed, either knowing ly or unknowingly, to change another's goods through deceit. From tummaroggi, comp. of mau and tattarroggi.

Mau-tattubboel
p162

互相來回地訪問

Mau-tattubboel, mi, ma, to visit each other backwards and forwards.

Mautattis
p162

拒絕，放棄

Mautattis, to reject, to abandon, as kar tattis, mi, ma, autatisa, autattisan, inautattis, inoautattisan. Pautattis, trans, but includes changes.

Mautod
p162

不結果實的，不成功的

Mautod, unfruitful, spoken as well of beasts as men. Also fruitless, as people give up anything that is fruitless.Pautod, trans. autod, unfruitfulness; Ma-autod, unfruitful.

Mautsiri
p162

天真的，樸實的，無知的，無經驗的

Mautsiri, minautsiri, mamautsiri,artless, ignorant, inexperienced, imp, autsiri. Pautsiri, trans, Autsiri, ignorance, Ma-autsiri, an ignoramus, as maautsiri.

Mazibûllach
p162

違規的，不正確的，不適當的

Mazibdillach, foul, improper, mi, ma, aziballacha, trans, paziballach, maballach, mi, ma, aballacha, to be foul; nom. Ballach, all kinds of things. Ma-aballach, one who acts disorderly.

Mazibochor
p162

不舒服地躺著（沒有枕頭、被子等等）

Mazibochor, minazibochor, mamazibo chor, aziboehorra, to lie uncomfort ably, without pillow, coverlid, &c'

Mazichil
p162

悲傷的

Mazichil, minazichil, mamazichil, azi chilla, (the part: are not otherwise used than with respect to the persons who are lamented, and are formed not from the neuter, but from the active pazichil.) azichillan, inazichillan, ino azichillan, sorrowful. Pazichil, act. et trans. pi, pa, act. imp. trans. azichil la, ipazichilla, &c. to make sad. Pichil, sadness. Ma-achil, one who is sad.

Mazich-zich
p163

被嚴重地磨平的

Mazich-zich, that which is badly smooth ed and ironed out, mi, ma, azichzicha. Pazich-zich, nom. The root zimich zich, see in Z.

Matshis
p163

腌製，製鹽

Matshis, brackish, saltish, mi, ma, atshisa, patshies, act. to salt, trans. imp. "atshia, atshisin, inatshis, inoatshisin, ipatshisa, &c. Tshis, saltness. Atshis a salting. Ma-atshis, a salter.

Mazigingin
p163

跛行

Mazigingin, minazigingin, mamazigingin, aziginginna, to halt, to limp. Pazigingin, atzigingin, a halting. Maatsigingin, a halter.

Mazhies
p163

帶有敵意

Mazhies, minazhies, mamázhies, azhis-a, azhis-in, &c. to carry on enmity. Pazhies, pi, pa, ipazhies-a, &c. Azhies-in, an enemy. Azhies, enmity, whence karri or mau azhies. Ma-ázhies, an enemy.

Mazikoar
p163

跳，跳過某物

Mazikoar, minazikoar, mamazikóar, azi kóara, azikóarran, inazikoaran, to jump, to jump over any thing.

Mazikáp
p164

足夠的，充足的

Mazikáp, just, enough, sufficient. Ma atsikap, sufficient. Patsikap, trans.

Matsilo
p164

長的，高的

Matsilo, long, high. Tsilo, length, height. Patsilo, trams. Ma-atsilä, long.

Maziloch
p164

勤勞的

Maziloch, mi, ma, azilócha, diligent. Mazilóch a rima, dextrous. Pazilóch, trans. Ziloch, nom. Ma-aziloch.

p164

Mazimán, minaziman, mamaziman, azi manna, azimannan, &c. to lay up trea sures. Patsiman, trans. atsiman, a treasure. Ma-atsiman, a hoarder.

p164

因眼花或虛弱跌倒

Maziporriporri, minaziporriporri, ma maziporriporri, aziporriporria; to fall down through giddiness or weakness; spoken only of men and beasts.

Mazipi
p164

發怒，發出噪音

Mazipi, minazipi, mamazipi, azipia, to rage, to make a noise. Azipi, a row. Ma-azipi, a fury.

Mbarri
p164

站立

Mbarri, minobarri, manobarri, obárria, abarrian, to stand. Paubarri, transi. It is really mobarri, but the (o) is so pronounced that it is not heard.

Mbûkkas
p164

白色，空白的

Mbûkkas, white, blank. Bukkas, the u short.

Mbe
p164

走開，離開

Mbe, minobe, mamobe, obea, obean, inobean, to go away, to leave. It is mobe, but the (o) is bitten off short, so as not to be heard. Paube, trans. to drive away.

p165

Mbod, mienbod, máambod, the falling off of hair, or feathers.

p165

Mchab
p165

偷

Mchab, mienchab, maamchab, chabba, chabben, ienchab, inochabben, to steal; is also taken for máchab, in general.

Mchách, mienchach, maamchach, chacha, chach-en, ienchach, inochachen, to dream.

Me

Me
p165

做多餘的事情

Me, to do any thing superfluous: differs from barras, and bior.

Mé-aab
p165

在做某件事中領先/優於別人

Mé-aab, mineaab, mameaab, eaba, ea ban, inoaban, inoeaban, to precede a nother in doing a thing; hence meaab mabá, to know, before hand, meab paha, to preconceive. Meapattis, to foretell. From meaab-maba, nomen, aijaab-maba, foreknowledge. From meaab-nmita, nom. aijaab-mita, prescience. From meaab-pattite, nom. aijaab-patite, prophecy. From meeaab-merab, nom, aijaab-merab, predetermination. From meaab-meries, nom. aijaab-meries, preparation. And is in other cases

Medadórri

Medadórri, minedadorri, mamedadorri, edadórria, edadorrian, inedadorrian, inoedadorrian, to quarrel with another. Aidadorri, nom. quarreling. This word is compounded of mau or kar, and means to quarrel together, again and again. Ma-aidadorri, a quarreller.

Mekap
p167

Mekap, mime, mame, ekappa, pass. ekappaggete ja baros, the settling of birds, on trees, or houses, after their flight. This is the same as mikkap, pakap.

Mema

Mema, fat, any thing very fat. Ema, fatness.

Merien

Merien, minerien, mamerien, erina, eri men, inerien, inoerien, to do, to make, also to arrange between parties. We use it also for create. Pairien, to do, to make, to form, nom. subst, airien, a making, creation. Ma-airien, maker, creator; as ma-atap.

Meries

Meroos

Meroos, mineroos, mameroos. erósa, erósan, ineroos, ino-eróosen, to marry, to he united. Meroos o badda, erosan ja sini. Airoosan, a son in law. Tamau o airoosan, tanai o airoosan, father and mother in law. Pairo-os, to marry out, imp. airóosa, airoosan, inairosan, inoai rosan, &c. ipairosa, pass. ipairoos, &c.

Miach

Mialla

Wiialla, minialla, mamialla, jalla, jallan, iniallan, inojallan, to look at anything with attention, Aialla, observation, beholding.

Mián

Mián, miman, mámian, iánna, iannau, iniannan, inoiannan, the rest and relaxation, which the Favorlang people observe for several days, whenever a chief dies; also the proclamation of holy days.

Midárdar

Mikkáp

Mikkáp, mi, ma, means to hold on, to to cleave, is said of the birds, when after a flight they come and rest on a tree or house, because they hold on with their claws, and as it were cleave fast; imp. ikkappa. Paikap, to stick, to cleave, activ. et trans. aikap, nom.

Mikkil, minikkil, mamikkil, ikilla, ikillan, inikillan, inoikillan, to fear, to be afraid, also to gird one's self, to watch.

p174

清理房屋

Mitatsiel, to cleanse; mitatsiel o don, o ta, to cleanse the house, or the place. Ta Deos mutatsil o torro boa innai arapies, God cleanseth us from sin.

Mitebabo

仰望，向高處看

Mitehabo, minitebabo, mamitebabo, itebahoa, to look up high.

p174

Mitírpo, minitírpo, mamitírpo, itírpoa, to look down below.

Mitoch
p174

Mitoch, tough, not easily torn asunder.

Mittin
p174

Mittin, minittin, mamittin, ittinna, ittinnen, inittin, inoittinnen, to threaten any one hehind his back.

Mkách
p174

黃色，綠色

Mkách, yellow, green.

Mkákach
p174

蒼白的，像病人

Mkákach, pale, like sick people.

Mkár

嘶啞的

Mkár, hoarse. Inkár jiri, a hoarse throat

Mo-ab
p174

Mo-ab, minóab, mamoab, o-abba, to increase in number or size, to cause increase. See paſab.

Móab
p174

（產生比較級）

Móab, makes the comparative degree, as moab a mato, mario, greater, better.

Moár
p174

（食物）溫熱的；（病人）熱的；（臉）羞愧的，生氣的，臉紅的

Moár, spoken of food, means lukewarm; spoken of a sick person, it means hot; spoken of the face, it means ashamed, angry, or rather blushing: differs from matadach.

Móas
p174

走路

Móas, minoas, mamóas, óasa, oásan, imoasan, ino-oasan, to walk.

Moba
p175

Moba, minoba, mamoba, oba, drowsy, as mba.

Mobàrri
p175

站立

Mobàrri, same as mbárri, to stand.

Mobe
p175

來自或去往某地

Mobe, same as mbe, either from, or to one's place. Paûbe, pi, pa, ipaûbe, to drive away.

Mocharanna
p175

從病中恢復，痊愈

Mocharanna and mocharanna-channa, mi, ma, ocharanna-channa, pass. ocharanna-channan, recovery from sickness: the sickness, is mocharanna-channa, but the body. Ocharanna-channan. Paucharanna-channa, trans. Aûcharanna-channa, recovery.

Mochib
p175

Mochib, minochib, mamochib, ochibba: ochibben, inochib, ino-ochibbeu, to carry alone. Paûchib.

Modaraûdaû

整圓

Modaraûdaû, round as a circle, modaraûdaû ja eidas, the full moon.

Moddon
p175

房屋的三角形頂

Moddon, the gables of a house.

Módon
p175

Módon, minodon, mamódon, odóma, odómen, inodon, ino-odónnen, to harden one's self against any thing.

Moeda
p175

怎麽回事？

Moeda, mi, ma, oeda, oedan, inoeda, inooedan, how is it?

Mogarini

Mogarini, and mogarinigini, round like a ball, also to roll. Pass. written mogarini. From gummarinigini.

Mokibach

Mokibach, notched; mokibach o silok, the knife is notched; kibach, a notch; okibacha, neutr, see the root ma-aukibach, notched, adject. kummibach.

Mokikiet
p177

撕開，撕裂

Mokikiet, torn, from kummikiet, nai. ma, okikiedda, act. et trans. aukikied. pi, pa; aukikiedda, aukikieddan, inau kikieddan, inoaûkikieddan, ipauki kidda, pas. ipaukikieddan, &c. nom. kikied, a rent; ma-aukikied, rent.

Móddon
p177

承擔或提高載重（負擔）

Móddon, means to take up a burthen. Also to increase one's burthen, and generally to increase or double a per son's work, for the first people say. moddon o paûchiep, and moddon o pásabo; and for the second, moddon o pataap, or pairien.

Moláppa

Moláppa, minoláppa, mamoláppa. oláppa, olappan, &c. to wander, to err.

Molliol

Molliol, minólliol, mamólliol, olliélla, olliéllan, inolliállan, ino-olliollan, to help any one in a work for friendship sake, and not for pay. A-olli-ol, help, as aùlliol; ma-a-olli-ol, a helper, as ma-aulliol.

Molso

Molso, the stenchions or posts, which stand by the side of houses.

Momatas-ó, as matas-o.

p178

Momo, a mole, the people of Formosa consider these as poisonous, and will not approach them.

Mópat, minopat, mamopat, opatta, opatten, inopat, ino-opatten, to go to meet ope: otherwise written mpat, the (m) short, without a vowel. Hence simpat, as it were si (i. sossi, or sinossi) mpat.

Mórich
p179

生存，維持生活

Mórich, minorich, mántorich, oricha, orichen, &c. to live, to maintain one's life. Porich, trans, to support, feed, and maintain another, nom. porich, is not in use for being, but means maintenance, feeding.

Morich
p179

保持活著

Morich, mi, ma, oricha, neutr, has no noun, as morich, to keep alive. Porich, pi, pa, oricha, pass, orichen, inorich, ino-orichen, to feed. Aurich, a feeding; ma-aurich, a feeder. Paurich, pi, pa, ipaûricha, pass. ipáurich, inipaurich, inoipaûrich, to make lively; also to cure of disease.

Morich
p180

身體的成長

Morich, mi, ma, origha, the growing of the body, pas, orichan, &c. Aûrich, nom. a growing. Porich, idem, ût sûpra, to feed another. Hence maaurich, such a feeder. Paurich, ùt súpra, to provide for another.

Moriedda
p180

逃離原本屬於的地方

Moriedda, minoriedda, mamoriedda, oriedda, orieddan, inorieddan, inoorieddan, to run away from those to whom we belong, as parents, partners, village, &c., Pauriedda, ditto. The root is rummiedda: ma-auriedda, such a fugitive. Aûriedda, such a flight,

Osás
p186

髮綹，稻草人

Osds, the tresses of hair, whether worn by the Chinese or natives. Also the bushy tops of the long grass, which are tied together to frighten animals.

Otáttan
p186

Otáttan, otattea, to do things moderately.

Otaútattán
p186

Otaútattán, Otaûtattea, as otattan.

Pa
p186

表否定

Pa, a word of denial. Patzi, there is no fish. Joined with nouns, it means to make, as pacha-och, to make a grave.Also to do ary thing, as paûcho, to louse; but mixed with other words it means to cause to do, as Papiech, to cause to fight unjustly. Pabórra, to pacify; or to suspect or accuse any one, as pachab, to accuse of theft. Pachod, one who raises an unjust suspicion.

pa
187

用溫暖的手巾搓揉很痠的四肢

pina. papa. aû, pass. a-en, ina, inoa-en, to rub a sore limb with a warm handkerchief, &c.

pûarpa
187

加入任何的社群

pinûarpa, papûarpa, aarpa, ipa-arpa, ûarpanni, inûarpan, inoaarpanni, to join one's self to any society. Cho Abasshe pinaarpó Batshekan, those of Abasshe have joined with Batshekan. Paarpa o dippi, to weld iron together. Nota, paarpa requires that the ends come over or into one another. See summasoom.

para
202

跟〈某人〉在一起；陪伴

pinûra, papara, arû, arûn, inara, inoaran, to be with any one, to accompany; araosse ta Cabba oe, does Cabba keep company? Ara, a comrade, pas. aran, inaran, to be accompanied: this passive is used with respect to those who attend on any one, as Takaba aran o Takalla, i.e. Takabba is waited on by Takala; or Takaba inara o icho, i. e. Takabba is attended by him; and aran, is also taken for the person who serves, that is the servant and maid.

領養小孩

pinaraba, papûraba, ara, aran, inara, inoaran, from Para, to adopt as a child, also to give up for that purpose; in which case it is ipûraba-a, iparaba. Paraba, act. and trans. The child rûmmaka, takes another for his father. The real father lets the child be taken by another. Paraba choa, refers to those who take the child; it is also said Paraba, to take a child. An adopted father raba amosjiem. The real father iparabo. The child is called by the adopten father, aran.

Paûchar

呼吸

pinaûchar, papaûchar, aûchûrra, aucharran, inaûcharran, inoaûchûrran, to breathe. Paûûchar, pi, pa, ippaûcharra, ipaaûchar, inipaaûchar, to do so. Hence char, the breath, also aûchar, the Spirit.

In which case it is auchussan, inauchussan, innauchussan. Paaûchûs, pi, pa, ipaaûchussa, ipaaûchus, inipaaûchus, to cause or let leave off. &c. See Maûchus

pinaûrtatach, papaûrtatach, ipaûrtatach-a, ipaurtatach-a, ipaurtatach, inipaurtatach, inoipaurtatach, to scatter. act. paaûrtatach, pinaaûrtatach, papaaurtatach, pa. ipaaurtatacha, ipaaurtatach, inipaaurtatach, inoipaaurtatach, to cause to be scatterd, trans, front Mortatach.

Paûloûn

使成為奴隸

pinauloan, papauloan, aûloanna, aûloannen, inaûloan, inoauloannen, to make any one for a labourer or slave. Also to do thus, in which case it is ipadloanna, ipauloan, inipaûloan, inoipaûloan. Loan, victuals, a slave, also a quadruped. But whenever this word is used for a slave, it is always employed in a bad sense.

Paûrûs
221

pinaûrus, papaurûs, aurussa, aurussar, inaurussan, inoaurusaan, to cool, to refresh. Paaurus, pi, pa, ipaaurûssa, ipaaurus, to do so; trans. from Morus, which see.

Pausâ

得到離開的許可

pinaûsà, papausû, ipaûsà, inipaûsa, inoipausa, to give permission to go, also to order to depart. Really to let go, i. e. to order to go. Paausa, pi, pa, to do so, trans. from Mossa.

Pausâ-o

pinausa-o, papausa-o, ausa-o-a, ausaoon, inausa-o, inoausa-oon, to embrace with one arm. Paausa-o, pi, pa, ipaausa-oa, ipaausao, &c. to do so.

Pazikakapol

pinazikakapol. papazikakapol, azikakápolla. azikakapollan, inazikakápollan, to run in the way, also to do so, in which case it is ipazikakápolla, ipazikakápol, &c.

Pazinado

翻譯；詮釋

pinazinado, papazinado, azinadoa, azinadon, inazinado, inoazinadon, to interpret. Pazinado tarran, to show the way. Paazinado, pi, pa, ipaazinadoa, ipaazinado, inipaazinado, to cause to interpret, &c. Tummacho, ditto. Patacho, or pitto, ditto. nom. tattach-o, in the verb trans. and noun, used with kar and mau, as kar tattacho, mau tattacho. Azinado, an interpretation. Ma-azinado, an interpreter.

222

pinaziogga, papaziogga, aziogga, azioggan, also anni, and aijan, inazioggan, inoazioggan, to put on an under garment. Paaziogga, pi, pa, ipaaziogga, &c. to do so. Ogga, an under garment.

Pazipo

洗臉

pinazipo, papazipo, azipoa, azipoon, inazipoon, inoazipoan, the washing of the face. Paazipo, pi, pa, ipaazipoa, ipaazipo, inipaazipo, &c.

Pazhesima

早上

the morning, from sun rise to half midday.

Pchab

用衣服包住自己

pienchab, pabchab, bchabba. bchábban, bienchabban, to cover one's self with a wrapper. To cover one's self. See Pabechab.

Pea

給予

pineam papea, ipea, ipe-a, inipea, inoipea, to give; changed into ea, ean, inean, &c. it means to be presented. Paya, pinaya, papaya, ipaya, inipaya, inoipaya, to cause to be given; this is written Paia, pi, pa, to distinguish it from Paija, to lean backwards. Aija, a gift. Ma-aija, a giver.

Pe-edda

（為了請客而）準備食物

forms into tpea, as Pea, to prepare and dish up food and drink; in order to treat anyone.

Pébe

pinébe, papébe, bebéa, bebeén, binébe, inobebéen, bebea, to dissuade. Pabebe, pi, pa, ipabebe. to do thus.

Pebé

麵團

pinebé, papebé, ebéa, ebéan, inebéan, inoebéan, as pedarra. Paibe, pi, pa, ipáibea. Aibe, nom. Aibe o rarobo, dough, i.e. flour mixed with water.

Pechab

暗殺

pinechab, papechab, echábba, echabban, inechabban, inoechábban, to murder secretly. Paichab, pi, pa, ipaichábba, ipaichab, &c. to fo thus.

Pedûrra

（很多事物的）混合體

pi, pa, edarra, edarran, inedárran, inoedarran, when different things are mixed together, as machoraáb. Aidarra; original substance with which anything is mixed, is edarran. Two different things, pedárra. A man, paidárra.

Pe-eo

pi, pa, e-eoa, to dangle. Pai-eo, trans. E-eo, one who swings.

Pees

pi, pa, eesá, pass. eesán, ineesan, inoeesan, to file; Paees, trans. Aees, a file; also steel, because they file with things in which there is much steel.

Peroa

pineroa, paperoa, éroa, eroan, ineroa, inoeroan, in two parts. Pairoa, pinairoa, papairoa, ipairoa, inipairoa, inoipairoa, to divide into two parts.

Pesasa

開始

pinesasa, papesasa, esasá, esásan, inesasa, inoesasan, to begin. Paisasa, pi, pa, ipaísasa, ípaisasa, &c. to be first to begin. Tackalla ja pesása ûmmop tûmmaapo bonna Tabaipaû ja rior. Tackalla has finished his field before Tabaipau. Aisasa, a beginning.

Pesasorri

改變（相似的事物）

pinesasorri, inesasorrian, inoesasorrian, to change similar things, but knowingly and on purpose, thus differing from Paûtatarrogi. Páisasorri, pi, pa, ipáisasorria, ipaisasorri, &c. thus to change.

Pesik

pi, pa, pesikkan, pass. pesikken, pinesikken, to break in pieces.

Pesil

pi, pa, pesilla, pesillen, pinesillen, inopesillen, is said of two fruits on one stalk, or when one root divides into two. Paisil, trans

Pesor

pinesor, papesor, esorra, esorrán, inesorranm, inoesorran, to mean, to imagine, to suspect. Paisor, pinaisor, papaisor, ipaisorra, ipaisor, inipaisor, inoipaisor, to imagine in general.

Pespûttil

分成四份

pinespattil, papespattil, espattilla, espattillen, inespattil. inoespattillen, to divide into four. Paispattil, pi, pa, ipaispattilla, ipaispattil, inipaispattil, inoipaispattil, to do so.

Petam

pinetam, papetam, etamma, etamman, inetamman, inoetamman, to lean upon the hand. Paietam, (to be distinguished from Paitam, to borrow,) pi, pa, ipaietûmma, &c. to do so.

Petórro

pinetórro, papetórro, etorroa, etorroan, inetorroan, inoetórroan, to divided into three. Paitorro, pinaitorro, papaitorro, ipaitorroa, &c. to do so.

Petûmmo

吐（ㄊㄨˇ）

pinetûmmo, papetummo, epetûmmoa, epetummo, inipetummo, inoipetummo, to spit upon. When it is also etûmmoa, etummoan, inetummoan, inoetummoan. Paitummo, pinaitummo, papaitummo, ipaitummoa, ipaitummo, &c. to do so.

Phon

(with an aspirate, not as fon,) the insects which eat out, and render hollow the bamboos.

Pia

現在

now; piada sisiá, to day.

Pía

驅逐野獸

pinia, papia, bia, bian, binia, inobian, to drive away the wild animals, such as hogs, and stags, who come and devour the fields. Babia, the nouns.

Píûch

piniách, pápiach, biácha, biachen, biniach, inobiachen, to separate fighters. Pabiach, pinabiach, pápábiach, ipábiacha, ipábiach, &c. to set apart.

Pian

拉（出）

pinian, popian, biárra, biárren, biniar, inobiarren, to pull out. Piar o bar, to lift up the arm. to strike. Pábiar, pinabiar. pa. ipábiarra, ipabiar, inipabiar, inoipabiar, to reach out.

Pichi

Pichír

(let the first i be scarcely heard) pinichir, papichir, bechirra, bechirren, binechir, inobechirren, to let go anything that is bent. Also to push away any thing into a stick. People say also Pichir o chacháap, to haul up a scoop net: pabichir, pi, pa, ipabichirra, ipabichir, inipabichir, inoipabichir, ditto.

227

piniéd, papied, bida, bidan, binidan, inobidan, to girdle. Pábied, pinabied, papábied, ipabida, ipabied, &c. to do so. Babied. a girdle. Babied an aijan, the place for the girdle.

Pigeno

Pigchillá

pi, pa, igchilla, pass. igchillán, &c. to put one thing between two others, where it does not adhere, but where it has room. Pichchárra, ditto. Paigchilla, trans. nom. aigchilla, the doing so. Chilla, lattice work.

Pilá

打

pinila2, papila, ilá, dán, inila, inoflan, to hit, to touch. Paila. Pinaila, papaila, &c. to touch. Thus people say, pila ja áúbo, the fish have got into the right basket, whenever there are fish therein. Aila, nom. a hitting.

Pilla
228

拆東西的工具

pinilla, papilla, billa, billaan, binilla, inobillaan, to cleave, to split. Babilla, pinabilla, pa2pabilla, ipabullá, &c. ditto. Babilla, a cleaving. Billa, a cleft from Malilla, anything to split with. Ma-ababilla, cleaver.

Pillála

常常拆開

pinillála, pi, pa, &c. to split frequently. Pabillabilla, &c. increases the sense. Pabilla, ditto.

Pillibilli

扭動

pinillibilli, papillibilli, billibilia, billibdien, hinillibilli, inobilliblien, binillibilli, inobilliblien. to turn around, act. to twist. Pabillibilli, &c. to cause to be twisted. Pillibilli o saris o aroot, thread, &c.

Pillíech

遮（？？）

pinilliech, seems to mean to put one's body in a position to do any thing imporatant. Pilliech o maûadet, o makarrieb,o tûmmaap, &c. to put one's self in a posture to pull out hair, to run, or to work. Pabilliech ditoo.

Pillik

？

intend. pillepillik, pi, pa, billika, billikken, binillik, inobillikken, to press or join anything underneath, (not between) as summiet. Pábillik, trans. babillik, nom. a pressing, also that which people lay on a thing to press it down.

Pióp

吹熄

pinióp, papióp, ioppa, &c. to blow up. Piop o chau, to blow the fire. Piop o tabillo, to blow up or in. Piop o tattallo, to blow out. Paiop, pi, pa, ipaioppa, ipaiop, &c. to do so.

Piór
229

遺留

pinior, papior, ipiórra, what? ipior, inipior, inoipior, to leave behind; to whom? biorran, bioiorrán, inobiorrán. Pábior, pi, pa, ipábiorra, ipábior, inipábior, inoipábior, to do so. Bior, a remainder, is also used as preposition.

Piri

搜尋；選擇；拒絕

piniri, papiri, iria, irian, inirian, inoirian, to search out, to choose, to reject, pairi, pináiri, ipairia, ipairi, to do so.

Pírbir

吹（蠟燭、火）

pi, pa, birbirra, birbirren, binirbir, inobirbirren, the blowing about of the flame of a fire or candle.

Pirraba

除草

irraba, irraban, &c. to weed, to pull up the weeds or grass out of the streets or places near the houses. But to weed fields is ummo-o; nevertheless this difference exists between the two, that Pirraba is used when people gather the weeds from amongst the good seed, but ummo-o when people pull up weeds out of a field, where no no good seed has been sown.

Pirras

撕裂

pinirras, papirras, pirrassa, pirrássen, pinirras, inopirrassen, to tear, act. Papirras, pinapirras, papápirras, ipapirrassa, ipapirras, &c. to do so.

Pirráas
230

(the i barely heard) the barley that is used in brewing liquor.

Pirroos

set on?

pinisor, papisor, isorra, isoninisor, inoisorren, to set on. Pis chau, to set on fire. Pisor o tazi, send up a kite. Paisor, pinai, papaisor, ipaisorra, ipaisor, inipai, inoipaisor, to cause to set on.

Pissárra

陪伴

Pinissárra, papissárra, issárran, inissarra, inoissarran, to ____ in to company. Páisarra, pinaisarra, papáisarra, ipaisarra, inipaisarra, inoipaisarra, ditto. Aissarra, an accompanying. Ma-aissárra, a _______ . Sarra, a lineal succession, where chiledren and grand-children follow each other. See below

Pissárrasárra

pi, pa, &c. when _____ follow one after the other, in the manner of the natives. Paissarrasarra, pi, pa, &c. to csuse _______ to be done.

Pissasson

休息

pinissássen, papissássen, issassena, issassenan, inisassenan, to rest. Paissassen, pi, pa, ipaissassena, ipaissassen, &c. to cause to rest. Aissassen, rest: aissassenan, time of rest; aissassenaihan, place of rest.

Pisse

矯正

pinisse, papisse, bissea, bissein, binisse, inobissein, to rectify. Pábisse, pinábisse, papábisse, ipábissea, ipábisse, &c. to cause to be rectified. Nom. Bisse, justice, righteousnesss. Babisse, rectitude, from Pisse. Abisse, a justifying; act. Passese; intentd. Pisse; nom. Bisse.

Pissillo

包覆

piensillo, papisaillo, bissilloa, bissilloan, biensillo, inobissilloon, to wrap up anything in order to take care of it, as, silk, money, tabacco, &c. Pábissillo, pi, pa, ipábissilloa, ipabissillo, &c. to cause to be done.

Pisso

抽出

(let the i be scarcely heard) pienso, pápisso, bissoá, bissoan, inobissoan, &c. to draw out, as people do i ndrawing lots, and all kinds of drawing. Pábisso, pi, pa, ipábissoa, to cause to be drawn. Babisso, a drawing; this noun compunded with mau or karri signifies lots, because such are made by the drawing out of tickets. Maababisso, a drawer.

Pissir

快速闔上手掌

piensir, papissir, pissirren, piensir inopiensirren, to close the gand fast, to press anything with the hand. Papissir, pinapissir. papápissir, ipápissirra, ipapissir, inipapissir, inoipápissir, to cause the ahnd to be closed.

Pititil

剪/切東西

pinitítil, papititil, bietbitilla, bietbitillen, to break, cut, or slice a thing into small pieces; but is often used of things that are long, and _____ (which?) by many transverse sections may made smaller, as a bamboo. a fish plantain, &c. Paititil, pi, pa, ipaititilla, to cause this to be done.

Pittas

把東西/動物切成兩半

pi, pa, pittassa, pittassen, pitássen, inopittassen, to cut the hind legs of an animal in two, or sever anything in two.

Pittassir

pinittassir, papittassir, ittassirra, ittassirran, inittassirran, inoittassirran, to do anything by the side of another, as walking, standing, lying, sitting, &c. Paitassir, pinaitassir, paitassir, ipaitassirra, ipaitassir, to cause the above to be done.

Pittas-tassir

pinittas-tassir, papittas-ttas-tassira, ittas-tassirran, as palalat. Paitastassir, pi, pa, ipaitas-tassirra, ipaitas-tassir, to do thus.

Pittátik

Pittaû

pi, pa, imp. ittaûa, to believe. Aittaûa, belief. Ma-aittaû, a believer.

Pittik

休息

pinittik, papittik, bittikka, bittikken, bientik, inobittikken, a pause in ____ (working? )when people have finished ____ . Also to rest one's self, from _____ of work, in order afterwards to work with new strength. pinitik, pinibittik, papábittik, ipábittikka, ipabittik, to cause to pause. pi, pa, bittoa, same as pazinado.

Pitto

as azinado.

Pittol

pinittol, papittol, ittollaen, ittóllia, ittollen or anai or aijan, initollan, inoittollan, to let anything alone, either while from despair of ever be able to reach the end. Páittol, pinaittol, papáittol, ipaittolla, &c. to cause this to be done.

Pizi

被強迫做某事

an expression by which it is meant that we are constrained to do something. Na a pizio. summarada, pizio na a man, na a pizi o merieo o bido. Pinizi, papizi, imp. Paizi, pinaizi. inipaizi, &c. to require any one to do anything, trans. izia, ipizia, pas, izian, &c.

Pizich

領導，帶領

pinizich, papizich, bizicha, bizichen, binizich, inobizichen, to direct; pizich o pach a, o mabarieb, o man, to lead on any one to fight, to run, to eat, &c. Pábizich, pi, pa, ipábizicha, ipábizich, o cause such to be done. Babizich, nom. a leading on. Ma-ababizich, a leader.

Po-pino
236

鳥叫聲

papo-poa, the cry and song of birds. Pábo, pinabo, papabo, ipaboa, ipabo, inipabo, inoipabo, to cause the birds to cry. Po, signifies also the cry of rats, mice, snakes, &c. Bábo, nom.

Poa

帶著水果

pinoa, papoa, imp. boa, to bring forth fruit. Páboa, pinaboa, papaboa, ipaboá, &c. to cause to bear fruit. Boa, nom. fruit, seed; person, flesh. Ma-ababoa, fruitful. Ma-ababoa o baron, a fruitful tree. But Poa, pi, pa, poá, pas. poán, pinoa, inopoan, to dye. Papoa, tans. papoa, nom the dying, and dye-stuff.

Ruiba

tsinarran, inotûrran: and **ban, inarriban, inoarriban: and rib**jen, rinibaijen, inoribaijen. Seems ** mean loathsome, or hurtful. Thus people speak of unusual food, arriban o ** macha ja micho. It is possible that it ** injurious or deadly. But these words require to be more carefully examined.

Tassinan
284

為某人做某事

tsinassinan, inotassinan, tassioa, to do anything for any one. Inatassinan ja rûmmozi-daû tamau, I will pay for my father. In the 2nd and 3rd person people do not say Tassinan, but Tassi. It is necessary that this word be examined. It is to be written tas-ina, just as daû-ina, for me; so also tasi-je, for you; tas-icho, for him. Præt. tsinas. fut. inosas, imp. tas ioa, sie d'r fas joa ina, take my place.

zinummanna, tatummanna, tanna, tanuaan, zinanna, inotannaan, to open. Tanna osja chachab o donoe, open the door of the house. Patanna, pi. pa. ipatanna, &c. to cause to open. Tattannanna o parara, an opening to let ** light, that is, a window.

Tûmmao
298

灑，如水、鹽

zinummao, tatummao, taoa, taoan, zinaoan, inotaoan, to sprinkle, as with water, salt thin m*d, &c. but to cover wood, stone, and other thhings that do not spread is magga. Wherewith * itaoon, inoitaoon. Patao, pinatao, papatao, ipatatoa, ipatao, inipatao, &c. to cause such to be done.

Tûmmara
300

tsi. tat. tara, taran, tsirara, inotaran, to choose anything first: as tummar' o mioa, tummar o mammali balach, to choose to cut down a field; to choose a lady. Patara, trans. ta*ara, a choice. Hence karri tatta-a, mau tat-ta-a, to choose one another.

Tûmmarad
300

zinummarad, tatummarad, taradda, taradden, zinarad, inotaradden, to gather up what another has scattered, as rice thrown over the floor. Patarad, pi. pa. ipataradda, ipatarad, &c. to cause wuch to be done.

tsi. tat. tamaramarra, tamaramarren, tsinaramar, inotaramarren, to be here and there, separated from one another, some here and some there. Pataramar, trans. such a scattering.

Tûmmaróggi
301

改變非常相似的事物，以至於人們很容易將它誤認為另一種，有意圖的欺騙

zinummaroggi, tatummaroggi, taroggia, taroggian. zinaroggian, inotaroggian, to change things which are so much alike that they can be easily mistaken one for the other, and this with intent to deceive. Pataroggi, pinataroggi, papataroggi, ipataroggia, &c. to cause such to be done.

Tumm*romma

tsi. tat. taromman, tsinaromman, inotaromman, to betray. Pataromma, trans. tattaromma, treachery. Hence karri-tattaromma, mautattanom-ma. Ma-atattaromma, a traitor.

Tummaroob
301

用扇子遮蓋住自己，以防日曬雨淋，沒有完全遮蓋住。或用地毯或類似物覆蓋，不同於 tummakkoob

zinummaroob, tatummaroob, tarroba, tarroban, zinarroban, inotarroban, to cover as people do the head with a fan, to pretect them from sun or rain: thus not entirely covered. Or to cover with a rug or such like in which it differs from tummakkoob. Tatarroob, pi. pa. ipatarroba, &c. to cause to cover.

Tûmmilla

zinummilla, tatummilla, itilla-a, initilla, inoitilla, to set in, to print in, to stick in, as people pierce a deer with a spear; or to imprint, as people press a seal on wax; while the impression is expressed by the pass. pret. of the verb initilla, that is, that which is impressed. Patillik, pinatillik, papatillik, ipatillikka, ipatillik, inipatillik, inoipatillik, to cause such to be done. Tûtillik, such a blinding.

Tummod

Tumpa
315

思考、反思

zinumpa, tatumpa, tuppa, tuppûan, zienpa, inotuppaan, to think, to reflect. Patuppa, pi, pa, ipatuppa, inipatuppa, inoipatuppa, to cause to to think. Tumpatuppa, intend. Tattuppa, thoughts. Maatattuppa, one who thinks.

316

zinumrach, tattumrach, tirracha, tirrachen, zinirrach, inotirrachen, the bursting of water through a dam. The escaping of a fish through a hole or rent in the net. The running out of paddy or such like article through a sack: the place where it leaks is tirrachan, zinirrachan, ino. &c. Patirrach, pi, pa, ipatirracha. &c.

Tsi
360

魚

fish. Tsi ballai, all sorts of small fish, catfish. Tsisàbbi, carp. I'si meried, eels. Tsi maarrát, shellfish. Tsi rodo, cod. Tsi tarra boetsina, a roach: tsi tarra pagaoûbaas, a sword fish. Tsi taiáûs, a sand-creeper. Tsi rócot, a smelt. Tsi teen, a fish, that has scales like the carp, but smaller. Tsi kabea, almost like the teen, but smaller. Tsi taddai, a sole. Tsi o bioog, a kind of sprat
